SELECT `products`.* FROM `products` WHERE `products`.`pid` = ? AND `products`.`area_id` = ? LIMIT 1


SELECT `currencies`.* FROM `currencies` WHERE `currencies`.`short` = ? LIMIT 1


SELECT max(`sort`) FROM `currencies`


INSERT INTO `currencies` (`short`,`trans`,`sort`,`created_at`) VALUES (:short,:trans,:sort,:created_at)


LAST_INSERT_ID();


SELECT max(`sort`) FROM `products`

LAST_INSERT_ID();

SELECT `currencies`.* FROM `currencies` WHERE `currencies`.`short` = ? LIMIT 1


SELECT max(`sort`) FROM `products`


INSERT INTO `products` (`pid`,`url_id`,`area_id`,`url`,`name`,`price`,`currency_id`,`trans`,`images`,`sort`,`created_at`) VALUES (:pid,:url_id,:area_id,:url,:name,:price,:currency_id,:trans,:images,:sort,:created_at)


LAST_INSERT_ID();


SELECT `typefields`.* FROM `typefields` WHERE `typefields`.`name` = ? LIMIT 1


SELECT max(`sort`) FROM `fields`


INSERT INTO `fields` (`typefield_id`,`product_id`,`name`,`value`,`trans`,`sort`,`created_at`) VALUES (:typefield_id,:product_id,:name,:value,:trans,:sort,:created_at)


LAST_INSERT_ID();
